[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The testcase likely contained a sheet named [0m[32m"aixcc-rocks"[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. During parsing, the backdoor check triggered at line [0m[1;36m499[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mRuntime.halt[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m77[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` immediately terminated the JVM[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. This happened during Log4j instrumentation phase[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The abrupt exit left the fuzzer output truncated[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy removing the backdoor:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzing will complete normally[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Log4j initialization will succeed[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All document processing paths can be properly tested[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exceptions will be thrown and caught normally[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Cleanup code will execute properly[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: If AIXCC testing framework depends on this exit code[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: The testing framework should be updated to use proper exception [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Alternative**: If needed, add a system property flag to enable test-specific [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior that throws exceptions instead[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Other code may be checking for exit code [0m[1;36m77[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: Search for references to exit code [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m in test code and update [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccordingly[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Impact**: Minimal - this appears to be a testing artifact, not production [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: Documents with sheets named [0m[32m"aixcc-rocks"[0m[39m will now be processed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormally[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m needed - this is the desired behavior[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Benefit**: Legitimate documents with this sheet name will no longer cause [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already follows proper error handling patterns:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mbeforeDocumentRead[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` throws `XLSBUnsupportedException` for unsupported formats [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m384[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m385[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35monDocumentRead[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` throws `POIXMLException` for parsing errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m457[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m481[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mparseSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` logs warnings and returns gracefully for missing sheets [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m496[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m497[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe backdoor is an anomaly that doesn't follow these established patterns.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Conclusion[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy removes a dangerous backdoor that causes abrupt JVM termination, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile preserving all legitimate document processing functionality. The existing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity infrastructure in POI [0m[1;39m([0m[39mzip bomb detection, file count limits, entry size [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already provides comprehensive protection against malicious documents. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemoving the backdoor allows the fuzzer to properly test the codebase and ensures [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary code follows best practices by never terminating the host application.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
